While this product doesn't do much for oil control, it keeps the skin hydrated and does not highlight any of my dry patches, as most foundations do. The extra hydration helps me be less oily anyway :)<br /><br />This product transfers easily, but this, again, can be fixed with some powder. It's definitely not full coverage either- if you have blemishes or dark spots, you will need concealer. However, it does wonders for evening out the skin tone and perfecting the skin in general.<br /><br />I'm 17, so I don't know how great it is for any signs of aging, but I do think it lives up to it's claims for providing intense nourishment and hydration while making the skin appear brighter and healthier.<br /><br />Overall, this product met my expectations. I would recommend this to anyone who is aggravated by dry skin, falls between the shades NC20 to maybe NC30 (might need powder), and doesn't want the makeup to be visible on the skin, even under scrutiny.

Also, as far as the claimed &#34;whitening&#34; effect: I tan pretty frequently and haven't noticed that my face looks any whiter than it normally does, but I have only been using the product for a few weeks now. It isn't moisturizing, but it also isn't too drying. I will say that it would probably emphasize dry skin/flakes without the use of an exfoliant and/or moisturizer beforehand.<br /><br />Over all, I really like this product. Hasn't caused me to breakout or any adverse skin irritation/reactions. It has silicone in it, so it acts as a primer as well (viz. pores minimized, etc.). It has SPF and a lot of good nutrients in it--I do feel my skin is overall healthier looking. I will DEFINITELY purchase this product again, though next time I'll try the SKIN79 Snail Nutrition BB Cream, since my skin does tend toward the dry side. So I ordered the pink and gold skin79 BB creams after researching dozens of BB creams(I'll admit, there were a few others which looked like they could be better than skin79's, but the bottle shape and color won me over HAHA)<br /><br />Little bit about me: Never used bb creams before, this is my first time ordering. Literally just got it out of the mail, only blended it on my hand, will update this when I start using it like tomorrow, but so far blends very well; I'm asian and have really pale skin and can't even tell it's on my arm!! There is a very light fragrant smell, the pink version feels more light than the gold, gold will probably be better for the dry winter time. I bought the gold version for my mom, but now that I look back the orange one seems it might be better for her skin, as it has higher SPF and she has a lot of sun spots on her cheeks.<br /><br />My delivery experience: I bought the 2 bottles from Pink Gelee, because I did not find any mixed comments about fake vs real products as SeoulGlamour/other sellers. After I ordered it, I immediately sent an email to Pink Gelee. I figured it wouldn't hurt to ask bluntly if they were real or not, and then I'd check it when the package came in. I received a reply promptly the next day, guaranteeing that their products are 100% guaranteed authentic. She even linked me a site to check the authenticity, and although that was reassuring I was not ready to give in the towel until I had the product in front of me and I could check for myself. The product came very promptly, first day of the estimated delivery date. (They are based in LA, and I live 30 minutes from there so that might be a factor to consider when ordering) Inside included a card saying thank you and a sample of the Pink and Gold versions, which was sweet (but I sorta just bought those 2... I kinda wished it was the orange vita plus sample :c )<br /><br />My overview on the authenticity: So it came in the mail today and I readily checked all the bookmarked links of how to tell if it's real or not. The thing though, about these photos are that Skin79 changes their packages regularly, probably to fool the people who are making fakes out there. The front label on the box and on the bottle says \\"Wrinkle Improvement\\" instead of Wrinkle Free. That freaked me out, because some of the 'Real' versions out there shows Wrinkle Free. Upon further studying and research, I found out that Skin79 recently changed their products to say Wrinkle Improvement, so +1 there. To all of you who just bought one recently and your bottle still says Wrinkle Free, :'( idk, check the date if it's 2012, should say Wrinkle Improvement! Also as a side note, those who say \\"oh, your product is fake if the labeled words scratch off,\\" that's just silly. Almost anything can be scratched off if it's out in heat, or dry areas long enough. I also found comments of a person who talked to a representative of cute and pretty, who sells authentic skin79 products, who even said that the label can scratch off, real or fake, if it's been let out in the sun or in different conditions long enough. So I think I'm going to skip that test, haha... not going to sit here and try to scratch off my brand new product to base if it's real or not.<br /><br />Second, the barcode should be on the bottom of the box; mine was on both products, as well as the expiration date and the manufacturing date. The manufacturing date was very recent as well, sometime this year, and expiration date in 2014. On the bottle itself there was also a sticker of authenticity, the gold version wasn't as nicely placed as the pink bottle.. it was slightly crooked, which made me worried. Perforated lines on both boxes were shown as well.<br /><br />Third, If you read inside the box, on the English part I found a typo: it said Wriinkle Improvement. I was like, damn, this is a fake. HOWEVER, after some research I found a lady who bought it full price from a local authorized retailer, and the real product also has this typo, which made me extremely relieved.<br /><br />Fourth, as a last check, I pumped a little on my hand. I've read that if it comes out leaky or watery, it's fake. It came out finely mixed, in one unison color and was lightly fragrant. The pink took like literally 20+ pumps to get it going, and the white only 1 or 2 pumps.<br /><br />After all this, I am almost sure now that the product I got was an authentic skin79 product. If you've kept up with me so far, hooray! You are now more informed! These are the elaborate reasons why I think my product is legit. I'll be buying from her from now on, unless someone finds new information to prove me wrong.

The drugstore brands in the US are decent for their price, but they're not nearly the same thing as the Asian-made BB's, nor do they carry the same benefits.<br /><br />This BB cream comes out a little greyish, but don't be disappointed. It oxidizes on your skin after about ten minutes to a much more natural color, but if you have a skin tone darker than a Fitzpatrick II (google it), this is not the product for you, because the color is pretty much only for light skins. Apply it and go brush your teeth or style your hair while it's setting to give it time to work.<br /><br /> This cream goes on easily - I just use my three middle fingers and pat it to blend. There's no streakiness and it's very easy to blend because it takes about five minutes to really set or &#34;dry&#34;. I don't have horrible acne, just the monthly crop, but I have issues with pigmentation and blotchiness from past issues, and this cream evens out about 80% of what I want to cover. I still go in with a mineral concealer and get the under eye darkness and any little spots that need more coverage, then finish with a powder to keep it all from shifting too much.<br /><br />As for the benefits: this BB cream (and pretty much every other one out there) claims to do tons of things, mainly correct, protect, and moisturize. It definitely protected my skin from sunburn when I was outside in the sun on a long photo shoot and my chest was burned (naughty me for not remembering sunscreen), and when I layer it with my mineral powder foundation, it gives about an SPF 40. Alone it's about a 20 or 25. The correction factor was awesome; much more than I expected and perfect for someone who wants a multi-use product or is just low-maintenance. The moisture factor was also good. It left my very dry skin dewy and cool, but it tends to crease really badly around my eyes, so if you have creasing issues, just be ready to check throughout the day and be ready to blend.<br /><br />In summary, I will absolutely be buying this product again. It's great for the price and looks fabulous on my models in the photo shoots I do, as well as in random shots on iPhones.
